begin machine
	dll MASTER.dll
	type 0
	begin gparam
		type 3
		id Volume
		desc Master Volume
		min 0
		max 0x4000
		no 0xFFFF
		flags 2
		default 0x2000
	end gparam
	begin gparam
		type 3
		id bpm
		desc Beats Per Minute
		min 0x10
		max 0x200
		no 0xFFFF
		flags 2
		default 126
	end gparam
	begin gparam
		type 2
		id tpb
		desc Ticks Per Beat
		min 1
		max 0x20
		no 0xFF
		flags 2
		default 4
	end gparam
end machine

		flags 2
		default 1
	end gparam
	begin tparam
		type 3
		id Length
		desc Length in length units
		min 1
		max 32768
		no 65535
		flags 2
		default 3
	end tparam
	begin tparam
		type 2
		id Length unit
		desc Length unit (0 = tick (default), 1 = ms, 2 = sample, 3 = 256th of tick)
		min 0
		max 3
		no 255
		flags 2
		default 0
	end tparam
	begin tparam
		type 2
		id Feedback
		desc Feedback (00 = -100%, 40=0%, 80 = 100%)
		min 0
		max 128
		no 255
		flags 2
		default 112
	end tparam
	begin tparam
		type 2
		id f. type
		desc Filter Type (0 = lowpass, 1 = highpass, 2 = bandpass, 3 = bandreject)
		min 0
		max 3
		no 255
		flags 2
		default 1
	end tparam
	begin tparam
		type 3
		id f. cutoff
		desc Filter Cutoff frequency in Hz
		min 10
		max 20000
		no 255
		flags 2
		default 550
	end tparam
	begin tparam
		type 3
		id f. bandwidth
		desc Filter Bandwidth (for bandpass and bandreject filters)
		min 1
		max 10000
		no 255
		flags 2
		default 100
	end tparam
	begin tparam
		type 2
		id Wet out
		desc Wet out (00 = 0%, FE = ~200%)
		min 0
		max 128
		no 254
		flags 2
		default 96
	end tparam
end machine

		default 1
	end gparam
	begin gparam
		type 3
		id Close Rate
		desc Close Rate
		min 1
		max 2000
		no 65535
		flags 2
		default 500
	end gparam
end machine
begin machine
	dll WhiteNoise StereoDist.dll
	type 2
	begin gparam
		type 2
		id Drive
		desc Pre distortion drive (-32 .. +64 db)
		min 0
		max 96
		no 255
		flags 2
		default 32
	end gparam
	begin gparam
		type 2
		id Top
		desc Top Threshold
		min 0
		max 248
		no 255
		flags 2
		default 254
	end gparam
	begin gparam
		type 2
		id Bottom
		desc Bottom Threshold
		min 0
		max 248
		no 255
		flags 2
		default 254
	end gparam
	begin gparam
		type 2

		desc Top Mode (Limit, Zero, Rectify, Pixelate, Saturate, Wrap)
		min 0
		max 5
		no 255
		flags 2
		default 0
	end gparam
	begin gparam
		type 2

		desc Bottom Mode (Limit, Zero, Rectify, Pixelate, Saturate, Wrap)
		min 0
		max 5
		no 255
		flags 2
		default 0
	end gparam
	begin gparam
		type 3

		desc Lowpass
		min 0
		max 1000
		no 65535
		flags 2
		default 1000

	begin gparam
